      <div class="container-fluid">
       <div class="row flex-xl-nowrap">
        <main class="mx-auto col-12 order-last" role="main">
         <div class="container py-3">
          <div class="row">
           <div class="col-sm-6">
            <div class="col-md-8 order-1 illo-container">
             <img alt="Get Connected" class="" src="../static/images/download/png/get-connected@3x.png?h=5e2656db">
             </img>
            </div>
            <h3 class="text-primary">
             Get connected
            </h3>
            <div class="row pl-3 pr-5 text-tpo">
             <p class="text-tpo">
              <span class="text-bold">
               If you are in a country where Tor is blocked, you can configure Tor to connect to a bridge during the setup process.
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="text-tpo">
              Select "Tor is censored in my country."
             </p>
            </div>
            <div class="row pl-3 pr-5 text-tpo">
             <p class="text-tpo">
              If Tor is not censored, one of the most common reasons Tor won't connect is an incorrect system clock. Please make sure it's set correctly.
             </p>
             <a href="https://support.torproject.org/en" title="Support Portal">
              Read other FAQs at our Support Portal
             </a>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="col-sm-6">
            <div class="col-md-8 order-1 illo-container">
             <img alt="Stay safe" class="" src="../static/images/download/png/stay-safe@3x.png?h=f11bdbfa"/>
            </div>
            <h3 class="text-primary">
             Stay safe
            </h3>
            <div class="row pl-3 pr-5 text-tpo">
             <p class="text-tpo">
              Please do not torrent over Tor.
              <br/>
              Tor Browser will block browser plugins such as Flash, RealPlayer, Quicktime, and others: they can be manipulated into revealing your IP address.
             </p>
            </div>
            <div class="row pl-3 pr-5 text-tpo">
             <p class="text-tpo">
              <b>
               We do not recommend installing additional add-ons or plugins into Tor Browser
              </b>
             </p>
             <p class="text-tpo">
              Plugins or addons may bypass Tor or compromise your privacy. Tor Browser already comes with HTTPS Everywhere, NoScript, and other patches to protect your privacy and security.
             </p>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>

              Tor Browser manual
             </u>

     <div id="site_status">
      <p>
       This page shows whether the site has been reachable and whether someone somewhere has been able to register, upload torrents, or post comments.
      </p>
      <p>
       If our sites have been available but you've been unable to reach them that is outside of our control. Some part of the Internet may have broken or someone may have deliberately blocked you.
       <br/>
       Give it a day or two then try a proxy or VPN.
      </p>
      <p>
       If our sites are down we'll already know and be working on getting them back up. We don't issue estimates so don't ask how long it will take.
      </p>

       https:
       <a href="https://thepiratebay.org">

             1.
             <div>
              <div style="height:20px;margin-bottom:2px; font-size: 12px">
               <input id="spoiler_title_Welcome to Suprbay" onclick="var spoiler_title = ('Welcome to Suprbay'.length) ? 'Welcome to Suprbay' : 'Show'; if (this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('div')[1].getElementsByTagName('div')[0].style.display != '') { this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('div')[1].getElementsByTagName('div')[0].style.display = '';this.innerText = ''; this.value = 'Hide'; } else { this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('div')[1].getElementsByTagName('div')[0].style.display = 'none'; this.innerText = ''; this.value = spoiler_title; }" style="font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; padding: 3px;" type="button" value="Welcome to Suprbay"/>

              <div class="alt2" style="margin: 0px; padding: 6px;">
               <div style="display: none;">
                <br/>
                a.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 What is this forum about?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                SuprBay is the official forum of The Pirate Bay. You can get help here for all of the Bay sites. Members use these forums as a way to communicate with others that have an interest in file sharing as well as to join in discussions.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                b.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 Who's in charge?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Every member of TPB or SB staff have a badge to indicate their position:
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <span class="mycode_size" style="font-size: x-large;">
                 Suprbay:
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <img alt="[Image: administrator.png]" class="mycode_img" src="https://pirates-forum.org/images/suprbay/administrator.png"/>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Administrators oversee the forum at the highest level.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <img alt="[Image: supermod.png]" class="mycode_img" src="https://pirates-forum.org/images/suprbay/supermod.png"/>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Super Moderators can moderate in any forum.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <img alt="[Image: moderator.png]" class="mycode_img" src="https://pirates-forum.org/images/suprbay/moderator.png"/>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Moderators generally have a specific forum (or several) that they are in charge of.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                For a full list, click
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://pirates-forum.org/showteam.php" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 here.
                </a>
                <br/>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>

               <div style="display: none;">
                <br/>
                a.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 Where should I post first?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Anywhere you like.
                <img alt="Smile" class="smilie smilie_1" src="http://suprbayoubiexnmp.onion/images/smilies/smile.gif" title="Smile"/>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                A good place to start is by
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://pirates-forum.org/Thread-Introduction-Thread-New-members-say-hi-here" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 introducing yourself and saying hello
                </a>
                .
                <br/>
                <br/>
                If you are
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 looking for a specific torrent
                </span>
                and would like help finding it then post in the
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://pirates-forum.org/Forum-Requests" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 Request forums
                </a>
                .
                <br/>
                <br/>
                If you need
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 help
                </span>
                with something or would like to start a
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 discussion
                </span>
                , then
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://pirates-forum.org/Forum-Member-Forums" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 post in one of these forums
                </a>
                .
                <br/>
                <br/>
                If you are an uploader and would like to
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 advertise your uploads
                </span>
                then
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://pirates-forum.org/Forum-Promote-Your-Torrents" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 start a thread in this forum
                </a>
                . (One thread per uploader)
                <br/>
                <br/>
                If you find a bug in
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 TPB
                </span>
                or
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 SB
                </span>
                , or need
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 help
                </span>
                with navigating then
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://pirates-forum.org/Forum-Site-Issues" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 start a new thread here
                </a>
                . Please search before starting new threads in the Site Issues forum, chances are that a thread already exists for the topic you wish to discuss.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                If you are having trouble logging in to
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 TPB or SB
                </span>
                or need help
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 changing
                </span>
                your
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 account details, or would like to discuss any matter relating to either your TPB account, your torrents, or your SB account
                </span>
                then
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://pirates-forum.org/Forum-Account-Issues" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 start a new thread here
                </a>
                . Note that members can create 1 thread only in the Account Issues forum, it is private and only yourself and staff/crew can view your thread.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                If you download
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 fake or infected torrents
                </span>
                then
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://pirates-forum.org/Forum-Report-Torrents-Comments" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 start a new thread here
                </a>
                . The Report Torrents/Comments forum is for reporting fakes, malware, child porn, mis-categorized torrents and/or spam. Note that the only threads you can see here are ones you have created.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                If you don't want to stay on topic, or you just feel like
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 letting loose
                </span>
                then join in one of
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://pirates-forum.org/Forum-The-Void" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 The Void
                </a>
                threads. Or start one of your own.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                b.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 Why is my post/thread in the Trashcan?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Moderators always give a reason when posts get moved to the Trashcan. Generally it falls into one of these circumstances:
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <span class="mycode_u" style="text-decoration: underline;">
                 Redundant threads
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Before making a new thread use the forum
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://pirates-forum.org/search.php" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 Search
                </a>
                and you might find that a thread already exists on that topic.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                If you make a thread that is too similar to an existing thread then it will be trashed.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <span class="mycode_u" style="text-decoration: underline;">
                 Frequently Asked Questions
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                If questions are asked often enough they are put into this document. Posting a thread asking a question that has already been answered here will result in your thread getting trashed.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <span class="mycode_u" style="text-decoration: underline;">
                 Thread Hijacks
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Posting on topic is important to maintain the viability of threads. If a thread's subject has nothing to do with you unique problem, posting about it in that thread is called 'Thread Hijacking'. It distracts the thread from its original subject and therefore the offending post will be moved to the Trashcan.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                c.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 How do I post?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Making new threads and posting replies is easy.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                When viewing threads just type into the Quick Reply box and click the Post Reply button, click the
                <img alt="[Image: newreply.gif]" class="mycode_img" src="https://pirates-forum.org/images/calm/english/newreply.gif"/>
                button to use the full editor or click the
                <img alt="[Image: newthread.gif]" class="mycode_img" src="https://pirates-forum.org/images/calm/english/newthread.gif"/>
                button when viewing forums to start a thread of your own.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                d.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 How do I correct a mistake in a post?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <img alt="[Image: postbit_edit.gif]" class="mycode_img" src="https://pirates-forum.org/images/calm/english/postbit_edit.gif"/>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                This button appears on every one of your posts. Click it and select between Quick Edit (a plain text editor right there in the post) or Full Edit with format options.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                e.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 How do I quote another post?
                 <br/>
                 How do I quote several posts?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                There are actually several built in ways to quote posts and also a manual method. It depends on what your intent is:
                <br/>
                <br/>
                To quote
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 one
                </span>
                post in the full editor - click this button on that post.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <img alt="[Image: postbit_quote.gif]" class="mycode_img" src="https://pirates-forum.org/images/calm/english/postbit_quote.gif"/>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                To quote
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 multiple
                </span>
                posts in the Quick Reply window, click this button on
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 all
                </span>
                the posts you would like to quote:
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <img alt="[Image: postbit_multiquote.gif]" class="mycode_img" src="https://pirates-forum.org/images/calm/english/postbit_multiquote.gif"/>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                When a post is selected for quoting, the above button looks like this:
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <img alt="[Image: postbit_multiquote_on.gif]" class="mycode_img" src="https://pirates-forum.org/images/calm/english/postbit_multiquote_on.gif"/>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                To enclose text from outside the forum in a quote format, just use the 'quote' tags.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                f.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 How do I format my posts with fonts and color?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Read this tutorial for more information on
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://pirates-forum.org/Thread-BBCodes-and-how-to-use-them" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 BBcodes
                </a>
                .
                <br/>

                g.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">

                </span>

                <br/>
                <br/>
                h.

                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://pirates-forum.org/usercp.php" rel="noopener" target="_blank">

                </a>
                and then click
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://pirates-forum.org/usercp.php?action=usergroups" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 Group Memberships
                </a>
                in the sidebar menu.
                <br/>
                <br/>

                <br/>
                <br/>
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 Warning:
                </span>

                <br/>

                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://chat.efnet.org:9090/?channels=thepiratebay.org&amp;uio=Mj10cnVlJjEwPXRydWUmMTI9dHJ1ZQ8a" rel="noopener" target="_blank">

                </span>

                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 What is an avatar?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>

                <br/>
                <br/>
                g.

                </span>

                </a>
                and click
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://pirates-forum.org/usercp.php?action=avatar" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 Change Avatar
                </a>
                .
                <br/>
                <br/>
                h.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">

                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>

                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://pirates-forum.org/Thread-SuprBay-User-Titles" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 this thread
                </a>
                .
                <br/>
                <br/>

'Getting Help' : 'Show'; if (this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('div')[1].getElementsByTagName('div')[0].style.display != '') { this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('div')[1].getElementsByTagName('div')[0].style.display = '';this.innerText = ''; this.value = 'Hide'; } else { this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('div')[1].getElementsByTagName('div')[0].style.display = 'none'; this.innerText = ''; this.value = spoiler_title; }" style="font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; padding: 3px;" type="button" value="Getting Help"/>

               </script>

              <div class="alt2" style="margin: 0px; padding: 6px;">
               <div style="display: none;">
                <br/>
                a. You may save yourself time by reviewing the
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://pirates-forum.org/Forum-Tutorials" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 Tutorials
                </a>
                before you type up a post and wait for a reply.
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://pirates-forum.org/search.php" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 Searching the forum
                </a>
                and
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://google.com/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 using Google
                </a>
                might also yield an answer.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                b. If you need help with TPB itself, post on our dedicated
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://pirates-forum.org/Forum-Site-Issues" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 Site Issues
                </a>
                forum.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                c. If you're feeling frustrated,calm down. We are volunteers, here to
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 help you
                </span>
                . We are
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 not here
                </span>
                for you to vent your anger on.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                d. The easier your question is to read, the more people are likely to read it, and answer it. So avoid typing in CAPS,
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 bold
                </span>
                , colour, or 1337/txtspk. Don't avoid spelling, grammar or paragraphs.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                e. Giving your thread a meaningful title will increase the chance of people who know the answer opening it.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                f. The more info you provide, the sooner we will be able to help you. Saves you waiting for us to ask you, then waiting again for us to read your reply. If you're having trouble with a torrent, post a link to it. If you're receiving an error message, tell us what it says. If you're stuck somewhere, tell us what you've done so far. etc.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                g. Finally, be patient. The one person who has the answer to your question may have gone to bed half an hour ago. Replies may take a while.
                <br/>
               </div>
              </div>

             1.
             <div>
              <div style="height:20px;margin-bottom:2px; font-size: 12px">
               <input id="spoiler_title_Welcome to The Pirate Bay" onclick="var spoiler_title = ('Welcome to The Pirate Bay'.length) ? 'Welcome to The Pirate Bay' : 'Show'; if (this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('div')[1].getElementsByTagName('div')[0].style.display != '') { this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('div')[1].getElementsByTagName('div')[0].style.display = '';this.innerText = ''; this.value = 'Hide'; } else { this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('div')[1].getElementsByTagName('div')[0].style.display = 'none'; this.innerText = ''; this.value = spoiler_title; }" style="font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; padding: 3px;" type="button" value="Welcome to The Pirate Bay"/>
               <script type="text/javascript">
                document.getElementById("spoiler_title_").value = "Show"; document.getElementById("spoiler_title_").id = "";
               </script>
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="alt2" style="margin: 0px; padding: 6px;">
               <div style="display: none;">
                <br/>
                a.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 What is The Pirate Bay?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Known as "The galaxy's most resilient BitTorrent site", "The world's largest digital library" or more simply TPB, The Pirate Bay is a Swedish file-sharing website founded in 2003 that hosts magnet links and has fought for the right to do so from the beginning.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Ranked perpetually as one of the top 100 most visited websites, TPB continues to grow and welcomes new members daily. The Pirate Bay has over six million registered users and as of May 2014, hosts over six million torrents.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Pirate_Bay" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Pirate_Bay
                </a>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                SuprBay is the official forum of The Pirate Bay.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                b.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 Who is in charge?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Each TPB staff member has a badge to indicate their position.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <img alt="[Image: Sn6VhGr.gif]" class="mycode_img" src="http://i.imgur.com/Sn6VhGr.gif"/>
                Administrators oversee TPB on the highest level. You will never see them, let alone speak to them.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <img alt="[Image: BFkwoaF.png]" class="mycode_img" src="http://i.imgur.com/BFkwoaF.png"/>
                Super Moderators are the rare case when a moderator doesn't die young.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <img alt="[Image: tpbsupermod.png]" class="mycode_img" src="https://pirates-forum.org/images/suprbay/tpbsupermod.png"/>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <img alt="[Image: VcjbpLT.gif]" class="mycode_img" src="http://i.imgur.com/VcjbpLT.gif"/>
                Moderators receive reports from Helpers and assist Super Moderators in daily tasks including bans (or lifting bans) and handling user accounts.
                <br/>
                <br/>

              <div class="alt2" style="margin: 0px; padding: 6px;">
               <div style="display: none;">
                <br/>
                a.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 What is torrenting?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Torrents are a way to share files. Take some time to read about torrents here:
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/BitTorrent" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 Wikipedia: BitTorrent
                </a>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                b.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 What do terms like torrent, peer, seed, swarm, tracker, etc. mean?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Any terms you need to understand should be listed in this glossary:
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Glossary_of_BitTorrent_terms" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 Glossary of BitTorrent Terms
                </a>
                .
                <br/>
                <br/>
                c.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 What software do I need?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                You need a "torrent client". There are many to choose from, here are some of the best:
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://www.utorrent.com/download.php" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 uTorrent
                </a>
                for Windows,
                <br/>
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://www.transmissionbt.com/download.php" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 Transmission
                </a>
                for Mac and
                <br/>
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://azureus.sourceforge.net/download.php?os=1" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 Vuze
                </a>
                for Linux.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                d.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 What are magnet links?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                When you download a torrent link, you actually get the torrent file from the site that you linked to. Magnet URIs allow you to obtain the torrent file from other users who are sharing the torrent in question.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                For more information about downloading with magnet links, see
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://pirates-forum.org/Thread-3010-Roll-your-own-magnet-links-if-your-proxy-is-fucking-with-the-real-ones?highlight=magnet+links" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 here
                </a>
                ,
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://piratebay.com.co/magnet-links/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 here
                </a>
                ,
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://torrentfreak.com/the-pirate-bay-says-goodbye-to-most-torrents-on-february-29-120213/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 here
                </a>
                , and
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://lifehacker.com/5875899/what-are-magnet-links-and-how-do-i-use-them-to-download-torrents" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 here
                </a>
                .
                <br/>
                <br/>
                e.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 How do I configure my torrent client for optimum performance?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Stop all your torrents and run
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://www.speedtest.net/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 this speed test
                </a>
                . If you're using uTorrent, select Options, Speed Guide and set the Connection Type to match the
                <span class="mycode_i" style="font-style: italic;">
                 upload
                </span>
                result. If you're using Vuze, use
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://infinite-source.de/az/az-calc.html" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 this calculator
                </a>
                to find what settings you will need to adjust.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                f.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 What port should I use?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Anything between 50000 and 65000 will be fine.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                g.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 Do I need to forward a port?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                It's a router function so if you don't have a router forget about it. If you do have a router you don't need to forward a port, you can download without doing so, but you will be able to connect to more people if you do. That can make a big difference when you are downloading from smaller swarms so it really is in your best interests.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                h.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 How do I forward a port?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                First, follow
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://www.portforward.com/networking/staticip.htm" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 this guide
                </a>
                to configure your computer to use a static IP address. Don't get confused with the static or dynamic IP address you are allocated by your ISP - your router uses that one. Then, follow
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://portforward.com/english/routers/port_forwarding/routerindex.htm" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 this guide
                </a>
                , selecting your router then your torrent client, to forward a port.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                i.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 How can I find out whether my ISP is throttling or blocking my torrents?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Run
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://broadband.mpi-sws.org/transparency/bttest.php" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 this test
                </a>
                .
                <br/>
                <br/>
                j.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 What can I do if my ISP is throttling or blocking my torrents?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Different ISPs employ different techniques but there are a number of things you can try. The most effective is likely to be switching to an alternative ISP or an alternative package from your current ISP.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                k.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 What can I do if my school is blocking my torrents?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Have someone off-campus download and burn discs for you, or download at home in the holidays. Don't even think of trying to circumvent the block - violation of network usage policies can lead to loss of internet access, suspension, or even expulsion.
                <br/>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
             <br/>

                f.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 What do the coloured skulls signify?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <img alt="[Image: trusted.png]" class="mycode_img" src="https://pirates-forum.org/images/suprbay/trusted.png"/>
                "Trusted" uploaders have had some of their torrents checked by Moderators who, so far, have found none containing fakes or malware. Those with Trusted status have a pink skull next to their name.
                <img alt="[Image: hC2084q.png]" class="mycode_img" src="http://i.imgur.com/hC2084q.png"/>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <img alt="[Image: vip.png]" class="mycode_img" src="https://pirates-forum.org/images/suprbay/vip.png"/>
                "VIP" uploaders are trusted uploaders who have stood the test of time. Those with VIP status have a green skull next to their name.
                <img alt="[Image: HvqDZI7.gif]" class="mycode_img" src="http://i.imgur.com/HvqDZI7.gif"/>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <img alt="[Image: UemkXn8.png]" class="mycode_img" src="http://i.imgur.com/UemkXn8.png"/>
                Those with blue skulls are "TPB Helpers" - members of the site staff responsible for identifying fake and infected torrents for the Moderators to delete.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                g.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 Can I have a pink skull?
                 <br/>
                 Can I have a green skull?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Don't ask - applications are
                <span class="mycode_i" style="font-style: italic;">
                 not
                </span>
                accepted and will
                <span class="mycode_i" style="font-style: italic;">
                 reduce
                </span>
                your chances. Just carry on uploading quality torrents and one day your skull will come. For further information, read
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://pirates-forum.org/Thread-ThePirateBay-Want-Trusted-VIP-Status-Pink-Green-Skull-See-Here" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 this thread
                </a>
                .
                <br/>
                <br/>
                h.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 Can I have a blue skull?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                TPB, from time to time, recruits users as TPB Helpers. Helpers assist the Mods on a daily basis, and those who are good enough will eventually move up to a Mod position. Don't ask to become a Helper. If we think you've got what it takes to join the crew, you'll get a tap on the shoulder...
                <br/>
                <br/>
                i.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 Where can I find a list of the torrents I've downloaded?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                You can't. The Pirate Bay doesn't record that information.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                j.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 Why do I get "Login failed"?
                 <br/>
                 Where have all my torrents gone?
                 <br/>
                 Where have all my comments gone?
                 <br/>
                 Am I banned?
                 <br/>
                 Why was I banned?
                 <br/>
                 Can you lift the ban?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                You can find out what happened and/or plead your case by creating a thread in the
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://pirates-forum.org/Forum-Account-Issues" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 Account Issues
                </a>
                forum. When you create a thread in Account Issues, be sure to complete the verification boxes at the top of the page (where it says Pirate Bay Username, Pirate Bay Password, then hit 'Validate.') to determine you're the account holder.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                k.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 Can you restore my torrents (now that you have lifted my ban)?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                No. Copies are not kept so you will have to re-upload them. Before you can do that you will need to post their hash values so we can clear them from our lock table. If you're using uTorrent or Vuze, hashes can be right-clicked on and copied from the General tab. They look like:
                <br/>
                <br/>
                470B3D9100362395C8B841B781AC3DDE4946F635
                <br/>
                or A8B8BAD1E2B4A287771774C7F396D8E6BFB466D5.

              <div class="alt2" style="margin: 0px; padding: 6px;">
               <div style="display: none;">
                <br/>
                a.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 What's wrong with Pirate Search?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                The Pirate Bay's search engine is not very reliable. If you're having trouble finding a torrent try adding an asterisk to your search phrase. If you're getting a lot of seemingly irrelevant results try changing the "Default sort order" under
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://thepiratebay.org/settings" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 Preferences
                </a>
                to "Uploaded (Descending)".
                <br/>
                <br/>
                You may find external sites do a better job indexing TPB than TPB does. Try searching on
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://www.u-torrent.eu/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 Torrentz
                </a>
                and clicking the "thepiratebay.org" link in the results. Or search on Google, using the
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 allintitle
                </span>
                and
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 site
                </span>
                keywords eg.
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://www.google.com/search?hl=en&amp;lr=&amp;safe=off&amp;q=allintitle:+watchmen+fxg+site:thepiratebay.org&amp;aq=f&amp;oq=&amp;aqi=" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 allintitle:watchmen fxg site:thepiratebay.org
                </a>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                b.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 Why hasn't &lt;insert title here&gt; been uploaded yet?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Because nobody has uploaded it here yet - torrents don't appear by magic. You could try searching on
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://torrentz.eu/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 Torrentz
                </a>
                ,
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://isohunt.com/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 isoHunt
                </a>
                (currently {10/2010} for users in the US this site is of limited use unless accessed
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://proxy.org/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 via proxy
                </a>
                ),
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://torrentreactor.net/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 Torrent Reactor
                </a>
                . You could also
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://pirates-forum.org/Forum-Requests" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 post a request
                </a>
                , including as much detail as you can so people will know exactly what you want. Do a search before posting in case there is an existing thread for the same request, and read the guidelines on the request forum index page.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                c.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 How can I avoid fakes and infected torrents?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Your judgement will improve with experience but
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://torrentfreak.com/stop-downloading-fakes-and-junk-torrents-071204/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 here
                </a>
                are some tips, and torrents from uploaders with icons next to their usernames eg.
                <img alt="[Image: hC2084q.png]" class="mycode_img" src="http://i.imgur.com/hC2084q.png"/>
                <img alt="[Image: HvqDZI7.gif]" class="mycode_img" src="http://i.imgur.com/HvqDZI7.gif"/>
                <img alt="[Image: UemkXn8.png]" class="mycode_img" src="http://i.imgur.com/UemkXn8.png"/>
                <img alt="[Image: VcjbpLT.gif]" class="mycode_img" src="http://i.imgur.com/VcjbpLT.gif"/>
                <img alt="[Image: BFkwoaF.png]" class="mycode_img" src="http://i.imgur.com/BFkwoaF.png"/>
                <img alt="[Image: Sn6VhGr.gif]" class="mycode_img" src="http://i.imgur.com/Sn6VhGr.gif"/>
                are safe bets. Please, if you are unlucky enough to download a bad torrent,
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://pirates-forum.org/Forum-Report-Torrents-Comments" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 report it
                </a>
                so a moderator can delete it.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                d.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">

                </span>

              <div style="height:20px;margin-bottom:2px; font-size: 12px">
               <input id="spoiler_title_Downloading" onclick="var spoiler_title = ('Downloading'.length) ? 'Downloading' : 'Show'; if (this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('div')[1].getElementsByTagName('div')[0].style.display != '') { this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('div')[1].getElementsByTagName('div')[0].style.display = '';this.innerText = ''; this.value = 'Hide'; } else { this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('div')[1].getElementsByTagName('div')[0].style.display = 'none'; this.innerText = ''; this.value = spoiler_title; }" style="font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; padding: 3px;" type="button" value="Downloading"/>

                document.getElementById("spoiler_title_").value = "Show"; document.getElementById("spoiler_title_").id = "";
               </script>
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="alt2" style="margin: 0px; padding: 6px;">
               <div style="display: none;">
                <br/>
                a.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 How can I comment on a torrent?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                You have to have
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://thepiratebay.org/register" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 registered
                </a>
                and
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://thepiratebay.org/login" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 logged in
                </a>
                before you can post a comment. Once you've done that a clickable "Write comment" link will be displayed next to the "Comments" field on the Torrent Details pages.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <img alt="[Image: 5ols64o.jpg]" class="mycode_img" src="http://i.imgur.com/5ols64o.jpg"/>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                b.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 Why does it say "Database error" when I submit a comment?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                There is a banned URL within your comment or the IP from which you are posting is banned.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                c.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 How can I complete downloading a torrent which is no longer being seeded?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                To ensure you can connect to any seeds: make sure you have a port forwarded, that you have enabled DHT and Peer Exchange, and that you are not using PeerGuardian or any IP blocking software. To find any more seeds: right-click and copy the Hash from the General tab and paste it into
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://torrentz.com/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 Torrentz
                </a>
                search to see whether it is being tracked by any other trackers. Finally, be patient - not everyone seeds 24/7 or at high speed, so just leave the torrent running.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                d.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 Why am I getting "Error: Not enough free space on disk"?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                This error occurs only on drives or partitions formatted to FAT32 because files greater than 4 GB cannot be created on FAT32 partitions. The only fix is to convert the drive or partition to NTFS, or use another drive or partition that is already using NTFS. To convert a drive to NTFS, read
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://support.microsoft.com/kb/307881" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 Microsoft's Knowledge Base article
                </a>
                .
                <br/>
                <br/>
                To ensure you can connect to any seeds: make sure you have a port forwarded, that you have enabled DHT and Peer Exchange, and that you are not using PeerGuardian or any IP blocking software. To find any more seeds: right-click and copy the Hash from the General tab and paste it into
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://torrentz.com/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 Torrentz
                </a>
                search to see whether it is being tracked by any other trackers. Finally, be patient - not everyone seeds 24/7 or at high speed, so just leave the torrent running.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                e.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 How likely am I to be caught?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                That depends on where you live, what you download, how much you download, who you're worried about being caught by (your ISP / a copyright holder / the police), whether you would consider a threatening letter being "caught" or if you would only count a court summons, etc. Overall, the chances of you being punished for downloading are statistically very low. But, they do exist -
                <span class="mycode_i" style="font-style: italic;">
                 only you
                </span>
                can decide whether they're worth it. Note that the risks are much higher if you torrent from school or work.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                f.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 How can I reduce the risk?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Blocklist tools, such as PeerGuardian, are ineffective. The only realistic way is to pay for access to a VPN such as
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://www.relakks.com/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 Relakks
                </a>
                . VPN's require the provision of large amounts of bandwidth so "free" VPN's are invariably short-lived and all VPN's suffer bandwidth constraints which result in slower than otherwise downloads.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                For a review of many popular VPNs look
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://pirates-forum.org/Thread-Which-VPN-Providers-Take-Anonymity-Seriously" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 here
                </a>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                g.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 What will happen to me if I am caught? /
                 <br/>
                 I've received a threatening letter, what should I do?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <span class="mycode_u" style="text-decoration: underline;">
                 Most
                </span>
                such letters say something along the lines of "We have received notification of an alleged copyright infringement...Copyright infringement violates our terms of service and may result in termination of your account." Note that the complaint originates from a copyright holder, not your ISP; and that your ISP does not reveal your identity to the complainant. You
                <span class="mycode_u" style="text-decoration: underline;">
                 should not reply
                </span>
                to any such letter (as a reply may be forwarded, thereby revealing your identity). Your ISP will rarely take any action against you--they prefer to continue receiving your monthly payments.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                If you're in the UK,
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://www.beingthreatened.yolasite.com/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 Being Threatened?
                </a>
                contains further information. If you're in the US,
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://www.chillingeffects.org/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 Chilling Effects
                </a>
                does likewise.
                <br/>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
             <br/>
             6.
             <div>
              <div style="height:20px;margin-bottom:2px; font-size: 12px">
               <input id="spoiler_title_Dealing with downloaded files" onclick="var spoiler_title = ('Dealing with downloaded files'.length) ? 'Dealing with downloaded files' : 'Show'; if (this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('div')[1].getElementsByTagName('div')[0].style.display != '') { this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('div')[1].getElementsByTagName('div')[0].style.display = '';this.innerText = ''; this.value = 'Hide'; } else { this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('div')[1].getElementsByTagName('div')[0].style.display = 'none'; this.innerText = ''; this.value = spoiler_title; }" style="font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; padding: 3px;" type="button" value="Dealing with downloaded files"/>
               <script type="text/javascript">
                document.getElementById("spoiler_title_").value = "Show"; document.getElementById("spoiler_title_").id = "";
               </script>
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="alt2" style="margin: 0px; padding: 6px;">
               <div style="display: none;">
                <br/>
                a.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 How do I open an ISO file?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                An ISO is a disc image which can either be burned to a physical disc using something like
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://www.imgburn.com/index.php?act=download" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 ImgBurn
                </a>
                "Write image file to disc" or mounted as a virtual disc using something like
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://www.daemon-tools.cc/eng/downloads" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 DAEMON Tools Lite
                </a>
                .
                <br/>
                <br/>
                b.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 How do I open an NFO file?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                An NFO is a text file containing information about the application / game / video contained within a torrent. They can be opened with a text editor (eg. Notepad) but will be easier to read if they are opened with a dedicated NFO viewer such as
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://www.softpedia.com/get/Office-tools/Text-editors/DAMN-NFO-Viewer.shtml" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 DAMN NFO Viewer
                </a>
                for Windows,
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://www.download.cnet.com/NFOViewer/3000-2079_4-82973.html" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 NFOViewer
                </a>
                for Mac, or
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://www.home.gna.org/nfoview/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 NFO Viewer
                </a>
                for Linux.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                c.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 How do I open a RAR file?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                They are archives which can be extracted with
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://www.rarlab.com/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 WinRAR
                </a>
                .
                <br/>
                <br/>
                d.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 How do I open R00, R01, R02,... (or 001, 002,...) files?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                They are a single archive which has been split, automatically, into multiple files; which will be joined, automatically, when you extract the first of them. They can be extracted with
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://www.rarlab.com/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 WinRAR
                </a>
                .
                <br/>
                <br/>
                e.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 Why can't I hear / see this video?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Your computer is missing a "codec" required to decode the audio and/or video part of the file you have downloaded. Installing the
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://www.cccp-project.net/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 Combined Community Codec Pack
                </a>
                if you're using Windows, or
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://perian.org/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 Perian
                </a>
                if you're using a Mac will usually solve the problem.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                If it does not, then open the file with
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://mediainfo.sourceforge.net/en" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 MediaInfo
                </a>
                for Windows or
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://mediainfo.massanti.com/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 MediaInfo Mac
                </a>
                to find out which codec(s) are required, and Google for them specifically.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                f.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 How can I watch an AVI file on a standalone DVD player?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                First, check whether the DVD player is "DivX Certified". If it is, you can burn as many AVI's as will fit onto a DVD using
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://www.imgburn.com/index.php?act=download" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 ImgBurn
                </a>
                "Write files/folders to disc".
                <br/>
                <br/>
                If it isn't, you really should consider purchasing one that is. Until you do you will have to convert the AVI files to DVD format before you burn them.
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://www.dvdflick.net/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 DVD Flick
                </a>
                is recommended for that and there is
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://www.dvdflick.net/guide/index_en.html" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 a tutorial
                </a>
                . Note that DVD Flick can burn as well as convert but it's safer to use it to create an ISO image and then burn that separately using
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://www.imgburn.com/index.php?act=download" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 ImgBurn
                </a>
                "Write image file to disc".
                <br/>
                <br/>
                g.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 Why am I asked to insert an "original" disk whenever I run my virtual or burnt CD/DVD?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                The game/app contains a copy-protection mechanism. Your download probably contained a "No CD/No DVD" crack which you will need to apply. If it does not, you might be able to find one at
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://www.gamecopyworld.com/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 GameCopyWorld
                </a>
                .
                <br/>
                <br/>
                h.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 Does The Pirate Bay require me to authenticate my account when downloading or running files?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Never. You don't need to register an account with TPB in order to browse/download, so TPB will never ask you for your log in information when you download or install something.  If you ever see a fake pirate bay pop up box asking for your username and password, ignore it, delete the file as it's fake and most likely riddled with trojans, and report the offending torrent in the Report Torrents section of the forum to crew. If you've downloaded malware, please reread Part 4: Finding Torrents &gt; c. How can I avoid fakes and infected torrents?
                <br/>
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
             <br/>
             7.
             <div>
              <div style="height:20px;margin-bottom:2px; font-size: 12px">
               <input id="spoiler_title_Uploading" onclick="var spoiler_title = ('Uploading'.length) ? 'Uploading' : 'Show'; if (this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('div')[1].getElementsByTagName('div')[0].style.display != '') { this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('div')[1].getElementsByTagName('div')[0].style.display = '';this.innerText = ''; this.value = 'Hide'; } else { this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('div')[1].getElementsByTagName('div')[0].style.display = 'none'; this.innerText = ''; this.value = spoiler_title; }" style="font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; padding: 3px;" type="button" value="Uploading"/>
               <script type="text/javascript">
                document.getElementById("spoiler_title_").value = "Show"; document.getElementById("spoiler_title_").id = "";
               </script>
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="alt2" style="margin: 0px; padding: 6px;">
               <div style="display: none;">
                <br/>
                a.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 How do I create and upload a torrent?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Follow
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://pirates-forum.org/Thread-2010-How-to-create-and-upload-a-torrent-using-uTorrent" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 this tutorial
                </a>
                if you're using uTorrent/BitTorrent or
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://pirates-forum.org/Thread-2020-How-to-create-a-torrent-and-upload-it-to-TPB-in-Vuze" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 this one
                </a>
                if you're using Azureus/Vuze.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                b.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 Why does it say "Wrong image code, the image code is a 9 letter long code from
                 <a class="mycode_url" href="http://bayimg.com/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                  http://bayimg.com/
                 </a>
                 "?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                You need to type the 5 letters shown in the captcha image into the "Enter code from image field" NOT into the "Image tag from bayimg" field.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <img alt="[Image: EPUhkx2.jpg]" class="mycode_img" src="http://i.imgur.com/EPUhkx2.jpg"/>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                c.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 Why does it say "Error (2) The torrent file seems to be broken"?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                There is a 0-byte file within your torrent. Remove any such files and recreate your torrent.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                d.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 Why can't I upload with Chrome?
                 <br/>
                 Why doesn't the Captcha display when uploading with Chrome?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                As of version 21 Google Chrome silently blocks elements that are not secure when they appear on a secure page.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Add the suffix - allow-running-insecure-content to your Google Chrome shortcut to permanently allow the mixed content to show in your browser.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Click the shield that appears in the omnibox URL bar when you visit the page where the Captcha should appear to allow the Captcha to show on a per page basis.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <img alt="[Image: YljM7w7.png]" class="mycode_img" src="http://i.imgur.com/YljM7w7.png"/>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                e.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 How can I update my torrent on the site?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                To modify the torrent itself is not possible, but if you wish to edit the torrent description, title, or correct a mistake you've made, you may ask tpb staff to edit/delete it for you, in your Account Issues thread.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                To upload the torrent again you need to post a request to have the hash cleared
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://pirates-forum.org/Forum-Account-Issues" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 here
                </a>
                .
                <br/>
                <br/>
                To modify the files within the torrent is not possible - that would change the torrent hash breaking compatibility with the existing swarm.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                To modify the trackers within the torrent is not supported by TPB.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                f.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 How can I delete my torrent from the site?
                 <br/>
                 I clicked the red 'X' and nothing happened. What gives?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                You can delete your own torrent by clicking on the red 'X' to the right hand side of it, above the title. If it appears that nothing has happened, or you are suddenly logged out (a glitch), try refreshing the page to see if the torrent is there. You may also request that the torrent be deleted in your Account Issues thread. Make sure you provide a link to the torrent/s you want deleting by posting the url link (not the delete link) in your thread, as well as the hash value if you want to reupload the torrent.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                g.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 I'm seeding my torrent, how come everyone is stuck at 99%?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://pirates-forum.org/Thread-4000-Seeding-but-nobody-completing-What-to-do" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 Read this
                </a>
                .
                <br/>
                <br/>
                h.
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 How do I "Re-Seed"?
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Follow
                <a class="mycode_url" href="http://forum.utorrent.com/topic/79972-how-to-reseed-a-file-i-already-removed/" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 this tutorial
                </a>
                if you're using uTorrent or
                <a class="mycode_url" href="https://wiki.vuze.com/w/Seed_an_existing_file" rel="noopener" target="_blank">
                 this one
                </a>
                if you're using Azureus/Vuze.
                <br/>
               </div>
              </div>

              <div class="alt2" style="margin: 0px; padding: 6px;">
               <div style="display: none;">
                <br/>
                Please use a
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 <span class="mycode_color" style="color: #ff3333;">
                  clean
                 </span>
                </span>
                image host free from pop ups, pop unders redirects and Full page (interstitial) ads.
                <br/>
                <br/>
                Only link directly to a clean image host, no third party links (eg. Linking to Extratorrent or 1337x where the viewer then is forced to click bad links)
                <br/>
                <br/>
                No URL shorteners to obfuscate bad links
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 Example of bad image host
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <img alt="[Image: Romanian_Girl.jpg]" class="mycode_img" src="http://s18.postimg.org/wf5tpywx5/Romanian_Girl.jpg"/>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 Example of Full page Interstitial Ad
                </span>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <img alt="[Image: fieldof_1.jpg]" class="mycode_img" src="http://s27.postimg.org/bk445no0j/fieldof_1.jpg"/>
                <br/>
                <br/>
                <span class="mycode_b" style="font-weight: bold;">
                 <span class="mycode_color" style="color: #ff3333;">
                  Anyone found using bad links will be banned from using thepiratebay.
                 </span>
                </span>
                <br/>

       <div class="row flex-xl-nowrap">
        <main class="mx-auto col-12 order-last" role="main">
         <div class="container py-3">
          <div class="row">
           <div class="col-sm-6">
            <div class="col-md-8 order-1 illo-container">
             <img alt="Get Connected" class="" src="../static/images/download/png/get-connected@3x.png?h=5e2656db">
             </img>
            </div>
            <h3 class="text-primary">
             Get connected
            </h3>
            <div class="row pl-3 pr-5 text-tpo">
             <p class="text-tpo">
              <span class="text-bold">
               If you are in a country where Tor is blocked, you can configure Tor to connect to a bridge during the setup process.
              </span>
             </p>
             <p class="text-tpo">
              Select "Tor is censored in my country."
             </p>
            </div>
            <div class="row pl-3 pr-5 text-tpo">
             <p class="text-tpo">
              If Tor is not censored, one of the most common reasons Tor won't connect is an incorrect system clock. Please make sure it's set correctly.
             </p>
             <a href="https://support.torproject.org/en" title="Support Portal">
              Read other FAQs at our Support Portal
             </a>
            </div>
           </div>
           <div class="col-sm-6">
            <div class="col-md-8 order-1 illo-container">
             <img alt="Stay safe" class="" src="../static/images/download/png/stay-safe@3x.png?h=f11bdbfa"/>
            </div>
            <h3 class="text-primary">
             Stay safe
            </h3>
            <div class="row pl-3 pr-5 text-tpo">
             <p class="text-tpo">
              Please do not torrent over Tor.
              <br/>
              Tor Browser will block browser plugins such as Flash, RealPlayer, Quicktime, and others: they can be manipulated into revealing your IP address.
             </p>
            </div>
            <div class="row pl-3 pr-5 text-tpo">
             <p class="text-tpo">
              <b>
               We do not recommend installing additional add-ons or plugins into Tor Browser
              </b>
             </p>
             <p class="text-tpo">
              Plugins or addons may bypass Tor or compromise your privacy. Tor Browser already comes with HTTPS Everywhere, NoScript, and other patches to protect your privacy and security.
             </p>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>

function dismissANN(id)
{

      <p>
       This page shows whether the site has been reachable and whether someone somewhere has been able to register, upload torrents, or post comments.
      </p>
      <p>
       If our sites have been available but you've been unable to reach them that is outside of our control. Some part of the Internet may have broken or someone may have deliberately blocked you.
       <br/>
       Give it a day or two then try a proxy or VPN.
      </p>
      <p>
       If our sites are down we'll already know and be working on getting them back up. We don't issue estimates so don't ask how long it will take.

             <br/>
             <div class="mycode_align" style="text-align: center;">
              <span class="mycode_size" style="font-size: x-large;">
               F.A.Q.
              </span>
             </div>
             <br/>
             <div class="mycode_align" style="text-align: center;">
              <span class="mycode_size" style="font-size: large;">
               This document is a list of frequently asked questions, their answers and a list of important tutorials.
              </span>
             </div>
             <br/>
             <span class="mycode_size" style="font-size: x-large;">
              <span class="mycode_color" style="color: #006400;">
               Suprbay
              </span>
             </span>
             <br/>
             <br/>
             1.
             <div>
              <div style="height:20px;margin-bottom:2px; font-size: 12px">
               <input id="spoiler_title_Welcome to Suprbay" onclick="var spoiler_title = ('Welcome to Suprbay'.length) ? 'Welcome to Suprbay' : 'Show'; if (this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('div')[1].getElementsByTagName('div')[0].style.display != '') { this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('div')[1].getElementsByTagName('div')[0].style.display = '';this.innerText = ''; this.value = 'Hide'; } else { this.parentNode.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('div')[1].getElementsByTagName('div')[0].style.display = 'none'; this.innerText = ''; this.value = spoiler_title; }" style="font-size: 14px; margin: 0px; padding: 3px;" type="button" value="Welcome to Suprbay"/>
               <script type="text/javascript">
                document.getElementById("spoiler_title_").value = "Show"; document.getElementById("spoiler_title_").id = "";
               </script>
